Se repartirán por igual”. ^[**30:24** Núm[ 31,27](ch046.xhtml#verse-1-Corintios-31-27)] [25]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-25 .bibleverse} Así fue desde aquel día y lo convirtió en estatuto y ordenanza para Israel hasta el día de hoy.
[26]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-26 .bibleverse} Cuando David llegó a Siclag, envió parte del botín a los ancianos de Judá, a sus amigos, diciendo: “He aquí un regalo para ustedes del botín de los enemigos de Yavé.” [27]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-27 .bibleverse} Lo envió a los que estaban en Betel, a los que estaban en Ramot del Sur, a los que estaban en Jattir, [28]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-28 .bibleverse} a los que estaban en Aroer, a los que estaban en Sifmot, a los que estaban en Estemoa, [29]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-29 .bibleverse} a los que estaban en Racal a los que estaban en las ciudades de los jeraelitas, a los que estaban en las ciudades de los ceneos, [30]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-30 .bibleverse} a los que estaban en Horma, a los que estaban en Borashan, a los que estaban en Athach, [31]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-31 .bibleverse} a los que estaban en Hebrón, y a todos los lugares donde David mismo y sus hombres solían quedarse.
\switchcolumn
\begin{english}

<h2 class="chaptertitle">[&nbsp;30&nbsp;](ch009.xhtml)<span><span id="chapter-1-Samuel-30"></span></span></h2>

[1]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-1 .bibleverse} When David and his men had come to Ziklag on the third day, the Amalekites had made a raid on the South and on Ziklag, and had struck Ziklag and burned it with fire, [2]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-2 .bibleverse} and had taken captive the women and all who were in it, both small and great. They didn’t kill any, but carried them off and went their way. [3]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-3 .bibleverse} When David and his men came to the city, behold, it was burned with fire; and their wives, their sons, and their daughters were taken captive. [4]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-4 .bibleverse} Then David and the people who were with him lifted up their voice and wept until they had no more power to weep. [5]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-5 .bibleverse} David’s two wives were taken captive, Ahinoam the Jezreelitess, and Abigail the wife of Nabal the Carmelite. [6]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-6 .bibleverse} David was greatly distressed, for the people spoke of stoning him, because the souls of all the people were grieved, every man for his sons and for his daughters; but David strengthened himself in Yahweh his God. [7]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-7 .bibleverse} David said to Abiathar the priest, the son of Ahimelech, “Please bring the ephod here to me.” 
Abiathar brought the ephod to David. [8]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-8 .bibleverse} David inquired of Yahweh, saying, “If I pursue after this troop, will I overtake them?” 
He answered him, “Pursue, for you will surely overtake them, and will without fail recover all.” 
[9]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-9 .bibleverse} So David went, he and the six hundred men who were with him, and came to the brook Besor, where those who were left behind stayed. [10]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-10 .bibleverse} But David pursued, he and four hundred men; for two hundred stayed behind, who were so faint that they couldn’t go over the brook Besor. [11]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-11 .bibleverse} They found an Egyptian in the field, and brought him to David, and gave him bread, and he ate; and they gave him water to drink. [12]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-12 .bibleverse} They gave him a piece of a cake of figs and two clusters of raisins. When he had eaten, his spirit came again to him; for he had eaten no bread, and drank no water for three days and three nights. [13]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-13 .bibleverse} David asked him, “To whom do you belong? Where are you from?” 
He said, “I am a young man of Egypt, servant to an Amalekite; and my master left me, because three days ago I got sick. [14]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-14 .bibleverse} We made a raid on the South of the Cherethites, and on that which belongs to Judah, and on the South of Caleb; and we burned Ziklag with fire.” 
[15]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-15 .bibleverse} David said to him, “Will you bring me down to this troop?” 
He said, “Swear to me by God that you will not kill me and not deliver me up into the hands of my master, and I will bring you down to this troop.” 
[16]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-16 .bibleverse} When he had brought him down, behold, they were spread around over all the ground, eating, drinking, and dancing, because of all the great plunder that they had taken out of the land of the Philistines, and out of the land of Judah. [17]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-17 .bibleverse} David struck them from the twilight even to the evening of the next day. Not a man of them escaped from there, except four hundred young men who rode on camels and fled. [18]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-18 .bibleverse} David recovered all that the Amalekites had taken, and David rescued his two wives. [19]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-19 .bibleverse} There was nothing lacking to them, neither small nor great, neither sons nor daughters, neither plunder, nor anything that they had taken. David brought them all back. [20]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-20 .bibleverse} David took all the flocks and the herds, which they drove before those other livestock, and said, “This is David’s plunder.” 
[21]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-21 .bibleverse} David came to the two hundred men, who were so faint that they could not follow David, whom also they had made to stay at the brook Besor; and they went out to meet David, and to meet the people who were with him. When David came near to the people, he greeted them. [22]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-22 .bibleverse} Then all the wicked men and worthless fellows of those who went with David answered and said, “Because they didn’t go with us, we will not give them anything of the plunder that we have recovered, except to every man his wife and his children, that he may lead them away and depart.” 
[23]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-23 .bibleverse} Then David said, “Do not do so, my brothers, with that which Yahweh has given to us, who has preserved us, and delivered the troop that came against us into our hand. [24]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-24 .bibleverse} Who will listen to you in this matter? For as his share is who goes down to the battle, so shall his share be who stays with the baggage. They shall share alike.” [25]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-25 .bibleverse} It was so from that day forward that he made it a statute and an ordinance for Israel to this day. 
[26]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-26 .bibleverse} When David came to Ziklag, he sent some of the plunder to the elders of Judah, even to his friends, saying, “Behold, a present for you from the plunder of Yahweh’s enemies.” [27]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-27 .bibleverse} He sent it to those who were in Bethel, to those who were in Ramoth of the South, to those who were in Jattir, [28]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-28 .bibleverse} to those who were in Aroer, to those who were in Siphmoth, to those who were in Eshtemoa, [29]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-29 .bibleverse} to those who were in Racal, to those who were in the cities of the Jerahmeelites, to those who were in the cities of the Kenites, [30]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-30 .bibleverse} to those who were in Hormah, to those who were in Borashan, to those who were in Athach, [31]{#verse-1-Samuel-30-31 .bibleverse} to those who were in Hebron, and to all the places where David himself and his men used to stay. 
\end{english}
\switchcolumn[0]*

<h2 class="chaptertitle">[&nbsp;31&nbsp;](ch009.xhtml)<span><span id="chapter-1-Samuel-31"></span></span></h2>

[1]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-1 .bibleverse} Los filisteos lucharon contra Israel, y los hombres de Israel huyeron de la presencia de los filisteos y cayeron muertos en el monte Gilboa. [2]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-2 .bibleverse} Los filisteos alcanzaron a Saúl y a sus hijos, y los filisteos mataron a Jonatán, Abinadab y Malquisúa, hijos de Saúl. [3]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-3 .bibleverse} La batalla fue dura contra Saúl, y los arqueros lo alcanzaron; y él se angustió mucho a causa de los arqueros. [4]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-4 .bibleverse} Entonces Saúl dijo a su escudero: “¡Saca tu espada y traspásame con ella, no sea que vengan estos incircuncisos y me traspasen y abusen de mí!” Pero su escudero no quiso, porque estaba aterrorizado. Por lo tanto, Saúl tomó su espada y cayó sobre ella. ^[**31:4** Jue[ 9,54](ch046.xhtml#verse-1-Corintios-9-54)] [5]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-5 .bibleverse} Cuando su escudero vio que Saúl estaba muerto, también cayó sobre su espada y murió con él. [6]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-6 .bibleverse} Así murió Saúl con sus tres hijos, su escudero y todos sus hombres aquel mismo día.
[7]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-7 .bibleverse} Cuando los hombres de Israel que estaban al otro lado del valle, y los que estaban al otro lado del Jordán, vieron que los hombres de Israel huían y que Saúl y sus hijos estaban muertos, abandonaron las ciudades y huyeron, y los filisteos vinieron y vivieron en ellas.
[8]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-8 .bibleverse} Al día siguiente, cuando los filisteos fueron a despojar a los muertos, encontraron a Saúl y a sus tres hijos caídos en el monte Gilboa. [9]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-9 .bibleverse} Le cortaron la cabeza, le despojaron de su armadura y enviaron a la tierra de los filisteos a todos los alrededores, para llevar la noticia a la casa de sus ídolos y al pueblo. [10]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-10 .bibleverse} Pusieron su armadura en la casa de Astarot, y sujetaron su cuerpo al muro de Bet Shan. [11]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-11 .bibleverse} Cuando los habitantes de Jabes de Galaad se enteraron de lo que los filisteos le habían hecho a Saúl, ^[**31:11** 1Sam[ 11,1-11](ch046.xhtml#verse-1-Corintios-11-1)] [12]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-12 .bibleverse} todos los hombres valientes se levantaron, fueron toda la noche y tomaron el cuerpo de Saúl y los cuerpos de sus hijos de la muralla de Bet Shan; llegaron a Jabes y los quemaron allí. [13]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-13 .bibleverse} Tomaron sus huesos y los enterraron bajo el árbol de tamarisco en Jabes, y ayunaron siete días. ^[**31:13** 2Sam[ 1,12](ch046.xhtml#verse-1-Corintios-1-12)]
\switchcolumn
\begin{english}

<h2 class="chaptertitle">[&nbsp;31&nbsp;](ch009.xhtml)<span><span id="chapter-1-Samuel-31"></span></span></h2>

[1]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-1 .bibleverse} Now the Philistines fought against Israel; and the men of Israel fled from before the Philistines, and fell down slain on Mount Gilboa. [2]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-2 .bibleverse} The Philistines overtook Saul and his sons; and the Philistines killed Jonathan, Abinadab, and Malchishua, the sons of Saul. [3]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-3 .bibleverse} The battle went hard against Saul, and the archers overtook him; and he was greatly distressed by reason of the archers. [4]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-4 .bibleverse} Then Saul said to his armor bearer, “Draw your sword, and thrust me through with it, lest these uncircumcised come and thrust me through and abuse me!” But his armor bearer would not, for he was terrified. Therefore Saul took his sword and fell on it. [5]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-5 .bibleverse} When his armor bearer saw that Saul was dead, he likewise fell on his sword, and died with him. [6]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-6 .bibleverse} So Saul died with his three sons, his armor bearer, and all his men that same day together. 
[7]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-7 .bibleverse} When the men of Israel who were on the other side of the valley, and those who were beyond the Jordan, saw that the men of Israel fled and that Saul and his sons were dead, they abandoned the cities and fled; and the Philistines came and lived in them. [8]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-8 .bibleverse} On the next day, when the Philistines came to strip the slain, they found Saul and his three sons fallen on Mount Gilboa. [9]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-9 .bibleverse} They cut off his head, stripped off his armor, and sent into the land of the Philistines all around, to carry the news to the house of their idols and to the people. [10]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-10 .bibleverse} They put his armor in the house of the Ashtaroth, and they fastened his body to the wall of Beth Shan. [11]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-11 .bibleverse} When the inhabitants of Jabesh Gilead heard what the Philistines had done to Saul, [12]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-12 .bibleverse} all the valiant men arose, went all night, and took the body of Saul and the bodies of his sons from the wall of Beth Shan; and they came to Jabesh and burned them there. [13]{#verse-1-Samuel-31-13 .bibleverse} They took their bones and buried them under the tamarisk^[**31:13** or, salt cedar] tree in Jabesh, and fasted seven days. 
\end{english}
\end{paracols}
